***money.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:money.html>money</a> (337)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology"><a href = vnd.unilang:etymology.html>Etymology</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">moneie</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">moneye</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:borrow.html>borrowed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href =
